    57	var log = istiolog.RegisterScope("gateway", "gateway-api controller")
    58	
    59	var errUnsupportedOp = fmt.Errorf("unsupported operation: the gateway config store is a read-only view")
    60	
    61	// Controller defines the controller for the gateway-api. The controller reads a variety of resources (Gateway types, as well
    62	// as adjacent types like Namespace and Service), and through `krt`, translates them into Istio types (Gateway/VirtualService).
    63	//
    64	// Most resources are fully "self-contained" with krt, but there are a few usages breaking out of `krt`; these are managed by `krt.RecomputeProtected`.
    65	// These are recomputed on each new PushContext initialization, which will call Controller.Reconcile().
    66	//
    67	// The generated Istio types are not stored in the cluster at all and are purely internal. Calls to List() (from PushContext)
    68	// will expose these. They can be introspected at /debug/configz.
    69	//
    70	// The status on all gateway-api types is also tracked. Each collection emits downstream objects, but also status about the
    71	// input type. If the status changes, it is queued to asynchronously update the status of the object in Kubernetes.
    72	type Controller struct {
    73	        // client for accessing Kubernetes
    74	        client kube.Client
    75	
    76	        // the cluster where the gateway-api controller runs
    77	        cluster cluster.ID
    78	        // revision the controller is running under
    79	        revision string
    80	
    81	        // status controls the status writing queue. Status will only be written if statusEnabled is true, which
    82	        // is only the case when we are the leader.
    83	        status *status.StatusCollections
    84	
    85	        waitForCRD func(class schema.GroupVersionResource, stop <-chan struct{}) bool
    86	
    87	        // gatewayContext exposes us to the internal Istio service registry. This is outside krt knowledge (currently), so,
    88	        // so we wrap it in a RecomputeProtected.
    89	        // Most usages in the API are directly referenced typed objects (Service, ServiceEntry, etc) so this is not needed typically.
    90	        gatewayContext krt.RecomputeProtected[*atomic.Pointer[GatewayContext]]
    91	        // tagWatcher allows us to check which tags are ours. Unlike most Istio codepaths, we read istio.io/rev=<tag> and not just
    92	        // revisions for Gateways. This is because a Gateway is sort of a mix of a Deployment and Config.
    93	        // Since the TagWatcher is not yet krt-aware, we wrap this in RecomputeProtected.
    94	        tagWatcher krt.RecomputeProtected[revisions.TagWatcher]
    95	
    96	        stop chan struct{}
    97	
    98	        xdsUpdater model.XDSUpdater
    99	
   100	        // Handlers tracks all registered handlers, so that syncing can be detected
   101	        handlers []krt.HandlerRegistration
   102	
   103	        // outputs contains all the output collections for this controller.
   104	        // Currently, the only usage of this controller is from non-krt things (PushContext) so this is not exposed directly.
   105	        // If desired in the future, it could be.
   106	        outputs Outputs
   107	
   108	        domainSuffix string // the domain suffix to use for generated resources
   109	
   110	        shadowServiceReconciler controllers.Queue
   111	}
   112	
   113	type ParentInfo struct {
   114	        Key  parentKey
   115	        Info parentInfo
   116	}
   117	
   118	func (pi ParentInfo) ResourceName() string {
   119	        return pi.Key.Name // TODO!!!! more infoi and section name
   120	}
   121	
   122	type TypedResource struct {
   123	        Kind config.GroupVersionKind
   124	        Name types.NamespacedName
   125	}
   126	
   127	type Outputs struct {
   128	        Gateways                krt.Collection[Gateway]
   129	        VirtualServices         krt.Collection[*config.Config]
   130	        ReferenceGrants         ReferenceGrants
   131	        DestinationRules        krt.Collection[*config.Config]
   132	        InferencePools          krt.Collection[InferencePool]
   133	        InferencePoolsByGateway krt.Index[types.NamespacedName, InferencePool]
   134	}
   135	
   136	type Inputs struct {
   137	        Namespaces krt.Collection[*corev1.Namespace]
   138	
   139	        Services   krt.Collection[*corev1.Service]
   140	        Secrets    krt.Collection[*corev1.Secret]
   141	        ConfigMaps krt.Collection[*corev1.ConfigMap]
   142	
   143	        GatewayClasses       krt.Collection[*gateway.GatewayClass]
   144	        Gateways             krt.Collection[*gateway.Gateway]
   145	        HTTPRoutes           krt.Collection[*gateway.HTTPRoute]
   146	        GRPCRoutes           krt.Collection[*gatewayv1.GRPCRoute]
   147	        TCPRoutes            krt.Collection[*gatewayalpha.TCPRoute]
   148	        TLSRoutes            krt.Collection[*gatewayalpha.TLSRoute]
   149	        ListenerSets         krt.Collection[*gatewayx.XListenerSet]
   150	        ReferenceGrants      krt.Collection[*gateway.ReferenceGrant]
   151	        BackendTrafficPolicy krt.Collection[*gatewayx.XBackendTrafficPolicy]
   152	        BackendTLSPolicies   krt.Collection[*gatewayalpha3.BackendTLSPolicy]
   153	        ServiceEntries       krt.Collection[*networkingclient.ServiceEntry]
   154	        InferencePools       krt.Collection[*inferencev1alpha2.InferencePool]
   155	}
   156	
   157	var _ model.GatewayController = &Controller{}
   158	
   159	func NewController(
   160	        kc kube.Client,
   161	        waitForCRD func(class schema.GroupVersionResource, stop <-chan struct{}) bool,
   162	        options controller.Options,
   163	        xdsUpdater model.XDSUpdater,
   164	) *Controller {
   165	        stop := make(chan struct{})
   166	        opts := krt.NewOptionsBuilder(stop, "gateway", options.KrtDebugger)
   167	
   168	        tw := revisions.NewTagWatcher(kc, options.Revision)
   169	        c := &Controller{
   170	                client:         kc,
   171	                cluster:        options.ClusterID,
   172	                revision:       options.Revision,
   173	                status:         &status.StatusCollections{},
   174	                tagWatcher:     krt.NewRecomputeProtected(tw, false, opts.WithName("tagWatcher")...),
   175	                waitForCRD:     waitForCRD,
   176	                gatewayContext: krt.NewRecomputeProtected(atomic.NewPointer[GatewayContext](nil), false, opts.WithName("gatewayContext")...),
   177	                stop:           stop,
   178	                xdsUpdater:     xdsUpdater,
   179	                domainSuffix:   options.DomainSuffix,
   180	        }
   181	        tw.AddHandler(func(s sets.String) {
   182	                c.tagWatcher.TriggerRecomputation()
   183	        })
   184	
   185	        svcClient := kclient.NewFiltered[*corev1.Service](kc, kubetypes.Filter{ObjectFilter: kc.ObjectFilter()})
   186	
   187	        inputs := Inputs{
   188	                Namespaces: krt.NewInformer[*corev1.Namespace](kc, opts.WithName("informer/Namespaces")...),
   189	                Secrets: krt.WrapClient[*corev1.Secret](
   190	                        kclient.NewFiltered[*corev1.Secret](kc, kubetypes.Filter{
   191	                                FieldSelector: kubesecrets.SecretsFieldSelector,
   192	                                ObjectFilter:  kc.ObjectFilter(),
   193	                        }),
   194	                        opts.WithName("informer/Secrets")...,
   195	                ),
   196	                ConfigMaps: krt.WrapClient[*corev1.ConfigMap](
   197	                        kclient.NewFiltered[*corev1.ConfigMap](kc, kubetypes.Filter{ObjectFilter: kc.ObjectFilter()}),
   198	                        opts.WithName("informer/ConfigMaps")...,
   199	                ),
   200	                Services:       krt.WrapClient[*corev1.Service](svcClient, opts.WithName("informer/Services")...),
   201	                GatewayClasses: buildClient[*gateway.GatewayClass](c, kc, gvr.GatewayClass, opts, "informer/GatewayClasses"),
   202	                Gateways:       buildClient[*gateway.Gateway](c, kc, gvr.KubernetesGateway, opts, "informer/Gateways"),
   203	                HTTPRoutes:     buildClient[*gateway.HTTPRoute](c, kc, gvr.HTTPRoute, opts, "informer/HTTPRoutes"),
   204	                GRPCRoutes:     buildClient[*gatewayv1.GRPCRoute](c, kc, gvr.GRPCRoute, opts, "informer/GRPCRoutes"),
   205

   602	
   603	// RouteResult holds the result of a route collection
   604	type RouteResult[I controllers.Object, IStatus any] struct {
   605	        // VirtualServices are the primary output that configures the internal routing logic
   606	        VirtualServices krt.Collection[*config.Config]
   607	        // RouteAttachments holds information about parent attachment to routes, used for computed the `attachedRoutes` count.
   608	        RouteAttachments krt.Collection[RouteAttachment]
   609	        // Status stores the status reports for the incoming object
   610	        Status krt.StatusCollection[I, IStatus]
   611	}
   612	
   613	type RouteAttachment struct {
   614	        From TypedResource
   615	        // To is assumed to be a Gateway
   616	        To           types.NamespacedName
   617	        ListenerName string
   618	}
   619	
   620	func (r RouteAttachment) ResourceName() string {
   621	        return r.From.Kind.String() + "/" + r.From.Name.String() + "/" + r.To.String() + "/" + r.ListenerName
   622	}
   623	
   624	func (r RouteAttachment) Equals(other RouteAttachment) bool {
   625	        return r.From == other.From && r.To == other.To && r.ListenerName == other.ListenerName
   626	}
   627	
   628	// gatewayRouteAttachmentCountCollection holds the generic logic to determine the parents a route is attached to, used for
   629	// computing the aggregated `attachedRoutes` status in Gateway.
   630	func gatewayRouteAttachmentCountCollection[T controllers.Object](
   631	        inputs RouteContextInputs,
   632	        col krt.Collection[T],
   633	        kind config.GroupVersionKind,
   634	        opts krt.OptionsBuilder,
   635	) krt.Collection[RouteAttachment] {
   636	        return krt.NewManyCollection(col, func(krtctx krt.HandlerContext, obj T) []RouteAttachment {
   637	                ctx := inputs.WithCtx(krtctx)
   638	                from := TypedResource{
   639	                        Kind: kind,
   640	                        Name: config.NamespacedName(obj),
   641	                }
   642	
   643	                parentRefs := extractParentReferenceInfo(ctx, inputs.RouteParents, obj)
   644	                return slices.MapFilter(filteredReferences(parentRefs), func(e routeParentReference) *RouteAttachment {
   645	                        if e.ParentKey.Kind != gvk.KubernetesGateway {
   646	                                return nil
   647	                        }
   648	                        return &RouteAttachment{
   649	                                From: from,
   650	                                To: types.NamespacedName{
   651	                                        Name:      e.ParentKey.Name,
   652	                                        Namespace: e.ParentKey.Namespace,
   653	                                },
   654	                                ListenerName: string(e.ParentSection),
   655	                        }
   656	                })
   657	        }, opts.WithName(kind.Kind+"/count")...)
   658	}
   659	
   660	// mergeHTTPRoutes merges HTTProutes by key. Gateway API has semantics for the ordering of `match` rules, that merges across resource.
   661	// So we merge everything (by key) following that ordering logic, and sort into a linear list (how VirtualService semantics work).
   662	func mergeHTTPRoutes(baseVirtualServices krt.Collection[RouteWithKey], opts ...krt.CollectionOption) krt.Collection[*config.Config] {
   663	        idx := krt.NewIndex(baseVirtualServices, "key", func(o RouteWithKey) []string {
   664	                return []string{o.Key}
   665	        }).AsCollection(opts...)
   666	        finalVirtualServices := krt.NewCollection(idx, func(ctx krt.HandlerContext, object krt.IndexObject[string, RouteWithKey]) **config.Config {
   667	                configs := object.Objects
   668	                if len(configs) == 1 {
   669	                        base := configs[0].Config
   670	                        nm := base.Meta.DeepCopy()
   671	                        // When dealing with a merge, we MUST take into account the merge key into the name.
   672	                        // Otherwise, we end up with broken state, where two inputs map to the same output which is not allowed by krt.
   673	                        // Because a lot of code assumes the object key is 'namespace/name', and the key always has slashes, we also translate the /
   674	                        nm.Name = strings.ReplaceAll(object.Key, "/", "~")
   675	                        return ptr.Of(&config.Config{
   676	                                Meta:   nm,
   677	                                Spec:   base.Spec,
   678	                                Status: base.Status,
   679	                                Extra:  base.Extra,
   680	                        })
   681	                }
   682	                sortRoutesByCreationTime(configs)
   683	                base := configs[0].DeepCopy()
   684	                baseVS := base.Spec.(*istio.VirtualService)
   685	                for _, config := range configs[1:] {
   686	                        thisVS := config.Spec.(*istio.VirtualService)
   687	                        baseVS.Http = append(baseVS.Http, thisVS.Http...)
   688	                        // append parents
   689	                        base.Annotations[constants.InternalParentNames] = fmt.Sprintf("%s,%s",
   690	                                base.Annotations[constants.InternalParentNames], config.Annotations[constants.InternalParentNames])
   691	                }
   692	                sortHTTPRoutes(baseVS.Http)
   693	                base.Name = strings.ReplaceAll(object.Key, "/", "~")
   694	                return ptr.Of(&base)
   695	        }, opts...)
   696	        return finalVirtualServices
   697	}

    40	type Gateway struct {
    41	        *config.Config `json:"config"`
    42	        Parent         parentKey  `json:"parent"`
    43	        ParentInfo     parentInfo `json:"parentInfo"`
    44	        Valid          bool       `json:"valid"`
    45	}
    46	
    47	func (g Gateway) ResourceName() string {
    48	        return config.NamespacedName(g.Config).String()
    49	}
    50	
    51	func (g Gateway) Equals(other Gateway) bool {
    52	        return g.Config.Equals(other.Config) &&
    53	                g.Valid == other.Valid // TODO: ok to ignore parent/parentInfo?
    54	}

    56	type ListenerSet struct {
    57	        *config.Config `json:"config"`
    58	        Parent         parentKey            `json:"parent"`
    59	        ParentInfo     parentInfo           `json:"parentInfo"`
    60	        GatewayParent  types.NamespacedName `json:"gatewayParent"`
    61	        Valid          bool                 `json:"valid"`
    62	}
    63	
    64	func (g ListenerSet) ResourceName() string {
    65	        return config.NamespacedName(g.Config).Name
    66	}
    67	
    68	func (g ListenerSet) Equals(other ListenerSet) bool {
    69	        return g.Config.Equals(other.Config) &&
    70	                g.GatewayParent == other.GatewayParent &&
    71	                g.Valid == other.Valid // TODO: ok to ignore parent/parentInfo?
    72	}

    74	func ListenerSetCollection(
    75	        listenerSets krt.Collection[*gatewayx.XListenerSet],
    76	        gateways krt.Collection[*gateway.Gateway],
    77	        gatewayClasses krt.Collection[GatewayClass],
    78	        namespaces krt.Collection[*corev1.Namespace],
    79	        grants ReferenceGrants,
    80	        secrets krt.Collection[*corev1.Secret],
    81	        domainSuffix string,
    82	        gatewayContext krt.RecomputeProtected[*atomic.Pointer[GatewayContext]],
    83	        tagWatcher krt.RecomputeProtected[revisions.TagWatcher],
    84	        opts krt.OptionsBuilder,
    85	) (
    86	        krt.StatusCollection[*gatewayx.XListenerSet, gatewayx.ListenerSetStatus],
    87	        krt.Collection[ListenerSet],
    88	) {
    89	        statusCol, gw := krt.NewStatusManyCollection(listenerSets,
    90	                func(ctx krt.HandlerContext, obj *gatewayx.XListenerSet) (*gatewayx.ListenerSetStatus, []ListenerSet) {
    91	                        // We currently depend on service discovery information not know to krt; mark we depend on it.
    92	                        context := gatewayContext.Get(ctx).Load()
    93	                        if context == nil {
    94	                                return nil, nil
    95	                        }
    96	                        if !tagWatcher.Get(ctx).IsMine(obj.ObjectMeta) {
    97	                                return nil, nil
    98	                        }
    99	                        result := []ListenerSet{}
   100	                        ls := obj.Spec
   101	                        status := obj.Status.DeepCopy()
   102	
   103	                        p := ls.ParentRef
   104	                        if normalizeReference(p.Group, p.Kind, gvk.KubernetesGateway) != gvk.KubernetesGateway {
   105	                                // Cannot report status since we don't know if it is for us
   106	                                return nil, nil
   107	                        }
   108	
   109	                        pns := ptr.OrDefault(p.Namespace, gatewayx.Namespace(obj.Namespace))
   110	                        parentGwObj := ptr.Flatten(krt.FetchOne(ctx, gateways, krt.FilterKey(string(pns)+"/"+string(p.Name))))
   111	                        if parentGwObj == nil {
   112	                                // Cannot report status since we don't know if it is for us
   113	                                return nil, nil
   114	                        }
   115	
   116	                        class := fetchClass(ctx, gatewayClasses, parentGwObj.Spec.GatewayClassName)
   117	                        if class == nil {
   118	                                // Cannot report status since we don't know if it is for us
   119	                                return nil, nil
   120	                        }
   121	
   122	                        controllerName := class.Controller
   123	                        classInfo, f := classInfos[controllerName]
   124	                        if !f {
   125	                                // Cannot report status since we don't know if it is for us
   126	                                return nil, nil
   127	                        }
   128	                        if !classInfo.supportsListenerSet {
   129	                                reportUnsupportedListenerSet(class.Name, status, obj)
   130	                                return status, nil
   131	                        }
   132	
   133	                        if !namespaceAcceptedByAllowListeners(obj.Namespace, parentGwObj, func(s string) *corev1.Namespace {
   134	                                return ptr.Flatten(krt.FetchOne(ctx, namespaces, krt.FilterKey(s)))
   135	                        }) {
   136	                                reportNotAllowedListenerSet(status, obj)
   137	                                return status, nil
   138	                        }
   139	
   140	                        gatewayServices, err := extractGatewayServices(domainSuffix, parentGwObj, classInfo)
   141	                        if len(gatewayServices) == 0 && err != nil {
   142	                                // Short circuit if it's a hard failure
   143	                                reportListenerSetStatus(context, parentGwObj, obj, status, gatewayServices, nil, err)
   144	                                return status, nil
   145	                        }
   146	
   147	                        servers := []*istio.Server{}
   148	                        for i, l := range ls.Listeners {
   149	                                port, portErr := detectListenerPortNumber(l)
   150	                                l.Port = port
   151	                                standardListener := convertListenerSetToListener(l)
   152	                                originalStatus := slices.Map(status.Listeners, convertListenerSetStatusToStandardStatus)
   153	                                server, updatedStatus, programmed := buildListener(ctx, secrets, grants, namespaces, obj, originalStatus, standardListener, i, controllerName, portErr)
   154	                                status.Listeners = slices.Map(updatedStatus, convertStandardStatusToListenerSetStatus(l))
   155	
   156	                                servers = append(servers, server)
   157	                                if controllerName == constants.ManagedGatewayMeshController || controllerName == constants.ManagedGatewayEastWestController {
   158	                                        // Waypoint doesn't actually convert the routes to VirtualServices
   159	                                        continue
   160	                                }
   161	                                meta := parentMeta(obj, &l.Name)
   162	                                meta[constants.InternalGatewaySemantics] = constants.GatewaySemanticsGateway
   163	                                meta[model.InternalGatewayServiceAnnotation] = strings.Join(gatewayServices, ",")
   164	                                meta[constants.InternalParentNamespace] = parentGwObj.Namespace
   165	
   166	                                // Each listener generates an Istio Gateway with a single Server. This allows binding to a specific listener.
   167	                                gatewayConfig := config.Config{
   168	                                        Meta: config.Meta{
   169	                                                CreationTimestamp: obj.CreationTimestamp.Time,
   170	                                                GroupVersionKind:  gvk.Gateway,
   171	                                                Name:              kubeconfig.InternalGatewayName(obj.Name, string(l.Name)),
   172	                                                Annotations:       meta,
   173	                                                Namespace:         obj.Namespace,
   174	                                                Domain:            domainSuffix,
   175	                                        },
   176	                                        Spec: &istio.Gateway{
   177	                                                Servers: []*istio.Server{server},
   178	                                        },
   179	                                }
   180	
   181	                                allowed, _ := generateSupportedKinds(standardListener)
   182	                                ref := parentKey{
   183	                                        Kind:      gvk.XListenerSet,
   184	                                        Name:      obj.Name,
   185	                                        Namespace: obj.Namespace,
   186	                                }
   187	                                pri := parentInfo{
   188	                                        InternalName:     obj.Namespace + "/" + gatewayConfig.Name,
   189	                                        AllowedKinds:     allowed,
   190	                                        Hostnames:        server.Hosts,
   191	                                        OriginalHostname: string(ptr.OrEmpty(l.Hostname)),
   192	                                        SectionName:      l.Name,
   193	                                        Port:             l.Port,
   194	                                        Protocol:         l.Protocol,
   195	                                }
   196	
   197	                                res := ListenerSet{
   198	                                        Config:        &gatewayConfig,
   199	                                        Valid:         programmed,
   200	                                        Parent:        ref,
   201	                                        GatewayParent: config.NamespacedName(parentGwObj),
   202	                                        ParentInfo:    pri,
   203	                                }
   204	                                result = append(result, res)
   205	                        }
   206	
   207	                        reportListenerSetStatus(context, parentGwObj, obj, status, gatewayServices, servers, err)
   208	                        return status, result
   209	                }, opts.WithName("ListenerSets")...)
   210	
   211	        return statusCol, gw
   212	}
   213	
   214	func GatewayCollection(
   215	        gateways krt.Collection[*gateway.Gateway],
   216	        listenerSets krt.Collection[ListenerSet],
   217	        gatewayClasses krt.Collection[GatewayClass],
   218	        namespaces krt.Collection[*corev1.Namespace],
   219	        grants ReferenceGrants,
   220	        secrets krt.Collection[*corev1.Secret],
   221	        domainSuffix string,
   222	        gatewayContext krt.RecomputeProtected[*atomic.Pointer[GatewayContext]],
   223	        tagWatcher krt.RecomputeProtected[revisions.TagWatcher],
   224	        opts krt.OptionsBuilder,
   225	) (
   226	        krt.StatusCollection[*gateway.Gateway, gateway.GatewayStatus],
   227	        krt.Collection[Gateway],
   228	) {
   229	        listenerIndex := krt.NewIndex(listenerSets, "gatewayParent", func(o ListenerSet) []types.NamespacedName {
   230	                return []types.NamespacedName{o.GatewayParent}
   231	        })
   232	        statusCol, gw := krt.NewStatusManyCollection(gateways, func(ctx krt.HandlerContext, obj *gateway.Gateway) (*gateway.GatewayStatus, []Gateway) {
   233	                // We currently depend on service discovery information not known to krt; mark we depend on it.
   234	                context := gatewayContext.Get(ctx).Load()
   235	                if context == nil {
   236	                        return nil, nil
   237	                }
   238	                if !tagWatcher.Get(ctx).IsMine(obj.ObjectMeta) {
   239	                        return nil, nil
   240	                }
   241	                result := []Gateway{}
   242	                kgw := obj.Spec
   243	                status := obj.Status.DeepCopy()
   244	                class := fetchClass(ctx, gatewayClasses, kgw.GatewayClassName)
   245	                if class == nil {
   246	                        return nil, nil
   247	                }
   248	                controllerName := class.Controller
   249	                classInfo, f := classInfos[controllerName]
   250	                if !f {
   251	                        return nil, nil
   252	                }
   253	                if classInfo.disableRouteGeneration {
   254	                        reportUnmanagedGatewayStatus(status, obj)
   255	                        // We found it, but don't want to handle this class
   256	                        return status, nil
   257	                }
   258	                servers := []*istio.Server{}
   259	
   260	                // Extract the addresses. A gateway will bind to a specific Service
   261	                gatewayServices, err := extractGatewayServices(domainSuffix, obj, classInfo)
   262	                if len(gatewayServices) == 0 && err != nil {
   263	                        // Short circuit if its a hard failure
   264	                        reportGatewayStatus(context, obj, status, classInfo, gatewayServices, servers, 0, err)
   265	                        return status, nil
   266	                }
   267	
   268	                for i, l := range kgw.Listeners {
   269	                        server, updatedStatus, programmed := buildListener(ctx, secrets, grants, namespaces, obj, status.Listeners, l, i, controllerName, nil)
   270	                        status.Listeners = updatedStatus
   271	
   272	                        servers = append(servers, server)
   273	                        if controllerName == constants.ManagedGatewayMeshController || controllerName == constants.ManagedGatewayEastWestController {
   274	                                // Waypoint and ambient e/w don't actually convert the routes to VirtualServices
   275	                                // TODO: Maybe E/W gateway should for non 15008 ports for backwards compat?
   276	                                continue
   277	                        }
   278	                        meta := parentMeta(obj, &l.Name)
   279	                        meta[constants.InternalGatewaySemantics] = constants.GatewaySemanticsGateway
   280	                        meta[model.InternalGatewayServiceAnnotation] = strings.Join(gatewayServices, ",")
   281	
   282	                        // Each listener generates an Istio Gateway with a single Server. This allows binding to a specific listener.
   283	                        gatewayConfig := config.Config{
   284	                                Meta: config.Meta{
   285	                                        CreationTimestamp: obj.CreationTimestamp.Time,
   286	                                        GroupVersionKind:  gvk.Gateway,
   287	                                        Name:              kubeconfig.InternalGatewayName(obj.Name, string(l.Name)),
   288	                                        Annotations:       meta,
   289	                                        Namespace:         obj.Namespace,
   290	                                        Domain:            domainSuffix,
   291	                                },
   292	                                Spec: &istio.Gateway{
   293	                                        Servers: []*istio.Server{server},
   294	                                },
   295	                        }
   296	
   297	                        allowed, _ := generateSupportedKinds(l)
   298	                        ref := parentKey{
   299	                                Kind:      gvk.KubernetesGateway,
   300	                                Name:      obj.Name,
   301	                                Namespace: obj.Namespace,
   302	                        }
   303	                        pri := parentInfo{
   304	                                InternalName:     obj.Namespace + "/" + gatewayConfig.Name,
   305	                                AllowedKinds:     allowed,
   306	                                Hostnames:        server.Hosts,
   307	                                OriginalHostname: string(ptr.OrEmpty(l.Hostname)),
   308	                                SectionName:      l.Name,
   309	                                Port:             l.Port,
   310	                                Protocol:         l.Protocol,
   311	                        }
   312	
   313	                        res := Gateway{
   314	                                Config:     &gatewayConfig,
   315	                                Valid:      programmed,
   316	                                Parent:     ref,
   317	                                ParentInfo: pri,
   318	                        }
   319	                        result = append(result, res)
   320	                }
   321	                listenersFromSets := krt.Fetch(ctx, listenerSets, krt.FilterIndex(listenerIndex, config.NamespacedName(obj)))
   322	                for _, ls := range listenersFromSets {
   323	                        servers = append(servers, ls.Config.Spec.(*istio.Gateway).Servers...)
   324	                        result = append(result, Gateway{
   325	                                Config:     ls.Config,
   326	                                Parent:     ls.Parent,
   327	                                ParentInfo: ls.ParentInfo,
   328	                                Valid:      ls.Valid,
   329	                        })
   330	                }
   331	
   332	                reportGatewayStatus(context, obj, status, classInfo, gatewayServices, servers, len(listenersFromSets), err)
   333	                return status, result
   334	        }, opts.WithName("KubernetesGateway")...)
   335	
   336	        return statusCol, gw
   337	}
   338	
   339	// FinalGatewayStatusCollection finalizes a Gateway status. There is a circular logic between Gateways and Routes to determine
   340	// the attachedRoute count, so we first build a partial Gateway status, then once routes are computed we finalize it with
   341	// the attachedRoute count.
   342	func FinalGatewayStatusCollection(
   343	        gatewayStatuses krt.StatusCollection[*gateway.Gateway, gateway.GatewayStatus],
   344	        routeAttachments krt.Collection[RouteAttachment],
   345	        routeAttachmentsIndex krt.Index[types.NamespacedName, RouteAttachment],
   346	        opts krt.OptionsBuilder,
   347	) krt.StatusCollection[*gateway.Gateway, gateway.GatewayStatus] {
   348	        return krt.NewCollection(
   349	                gatewayStatuses,
   350	                func(ctx krt.HandlerContext, i krt.ObjectWithStatus[*gateway.Gateway, gateway.GatewayStatus]) *krt.ObjectWithStatus[*gateway.Gateway, gateway.GatewayStatus] {
   351	                        tcpRoutes := krt.Fetch(ctx, routeAttachments, krt.FilterIndex(routeAttachmentsIndex, config.NamespacedName(i.Obj)))
   352	                        counts := map[string]int32{}
   353	                        for _, r := range tcpRoutes {
   354	                                counts[r.ListenerName]++
   355	                        }
   356	                        status := i.Status.DeepCopy()
   357	                        for i, s := range status.Listeners {
   358	                                s.AttachedRoutes = counts[string(s.Name)]
   359	                                status.Listeners[i] = s
   360	                        }
   361	                        return &krt.ObjectWithStatus[*gateway.Gateway, gateway.GatewayStatus]{
   362	                                Obj:    i.Obj,
   363	                                Status: *status,
   364	                        }
   365	                }, opts.WithName("GatewayFinalStatus")...)
   366	}
   367	
   368	// RouteParents holds information about things routes can reference as parents.
   369	type RouteParents struct {
   370	        gateways     krt.Collection[Gateway]
   371	        gatewayIndex krt.Index[parentKey, Gateway]
   372	}
   373	
   374	func (p RouteParents) fetch(ctx krt.HandlerContext, pk parentKey) []*parentInfo {
   375	        if pk == meshParentKey {
   376	                // Special case
   377	                return []*parentInfo{
   378	                        {
   379	                                InternalName: "mesh",
   380	                                // Mesh has no configurable AllowedKinds, so allow all supported
   381	                                AllowedKinds: []gateway.RouteGroupKind{
   382	                                        {Group: (*gateway.Group)(ptr.Of(gvk.HTTPRoute.Group)), Kind: gateway.Kind(gvk.HTTPRoute.Kind)},
   383	                                        {Group: (*gateway.Group)(ptr.Of(gvk.GRPCRoute.Group)), Kind: gateway.Kind(gvk.GRPCRoute.Kind)},
   384	                                        {Group: (*gateway.Group)(ptr.Of(gvk.TCPRoute.Group)), Kind: gateway.Kind(gvk.TCPRoute.Kind)},
   385	                                        {Group: (*gateway.Group)(ptr.Of(gvk.TLSRoute.Group)), Kind: gateway.Kind(gvk.TLSRoute.Kind)},
   386	                                },
   387	                        },
   388	                }
   389	        }
   390	        return slices.Map(krt.Fetch(ctx, p.gateways, krt.FilterIndex(p.gatewayIndex, pk)), func(gw Gateway) *parentInfo {
   391	                return &gw.ParentInfo
   392	        })
   393	}
   394	
   395	func BuildRouteParents(
   396	        gateways krt.Collection[Gateway],
   397	) RouteParents {
   398	        idx := krt.NewIndex(gateways, "parent", func(o Gateway) []parentKey {
   399	                return []parentKey{o.Parent}
   400	        })
   401	        return RouteParents{
   402	                gateways:     gateways,
   403	                gatewayIndex: idx,
   404	        }
   405	}
   406	
   407	func detectListenerPortNumber(l gatewayx.ListenerEntry) (gatewayx.PortNumber, error) {
   408	        if l.Port != 0 {
   409	                return l.Port, nil
   410	        }
   411	        switch l.Protocol {
   412	        case gatewayv1.HTTPProtocolType:
   413	                return 80, nil
   414	        case gatewayv1.HTTPSProtocolType:
   415	                return 443, nil
   416	        }
   417	        return 0, fmt.Errorf("protocol %v requires a port to be set", l.Protocol)
   418	}
   419	
   420	func convertStandardStatusToListenerSetStatus(l gatewayx.ListenerEntry) func(e gateway.ListenerStatus) gatewayx.ListenerEntryStatus {
   421	        return func(e gateway.ListenerStatus) gatewayx.ListenerEntryStatus {
   422	                return gatewayx.ListenerEntryStatus{
   423	                        Name:           e.Name,
   424	                        Port:           l.Port,
   425	                        SupportedKinds: e.SupportedKinds,
   426	                        AttachedRoutes: e.AttachedRoutes,
   427	                        Conditions:     e.Conditions,
   428	                }
   429	        }
   430	}
   431	
   432	func convertListenerSetStatusToStandardStatus(e gatewayx.ListenerEntryStatus) gateway.ListenerStatus {
   433	        return gateway.ListenerStatus{
   434	                Name:           e.Name,
   435	                SupportedKinds: e.SupportedKinds,
   436	                AttachedRoutes: e.AttachedRoutes,
   437	                Conditions:     e.Conditions,
   438	        }
   439	}
   440	
   441	func convertListenerSetToListener(l gatewayx.ListenerEntry) gateway.Listener {
   442	        // For now, structs are identical enough Go can cast them. I doubt this will hold up forever, but we can adjust as needed.
   443	        return gateway.Listener(l)
   444	}

    67	
    68	// DeploymentController implements a controller that materializes a Gateway into an in cluster gateway proxy
    69	// to serve requests from. This is implemented with a Deployment and Service today.
    70	// The implementation makes a few non-obvious choices - namely using Server Side Apply from go templates
    71	// and not using controller-runtime.
    72	//
    73	// controller-runtime has a number of constraints that make it inappropriate for usage here, despite this
    74	// seeming to be the bread and butter of the library:
    75	// * It is not readily possible to bring existing Informers, which would require extra watches (#1668)
    76	// * Goroutine leaks (#1655)
    77	// * Excessive API-server calls at startup which have no benefit to us (#1603)
    78	// * Hard to use with SSA (#1669)
    79	// While these can be worked around, at some point it isn't worth the effort.
    80	//
    81	// Server Side Apply with go templates is an odd choice (no one likes YAML templating...) but is one of the few
    82	// remaining options after all others are ruled out.
    83	//   - Merge patch/Update cannot be used. If we always enforce that our object is *exactly* the same as
    84	//     the in-cluster object we will get in endless loops due to other controllers that like to add annotations, etc.
    85	//     If we chose to allow any unknown fields, then we would never be able to remove fields we added, as
    86	//     we cannot tell if we created it or someone else did. SSA fixes these issues
    87	//   - SSA using client-go Apply libraries is almost a good choice, but most third-party clients (Istio, MCS, and gateway-api)
    88	//     do not provide these libraries.
    89	//   - SSA using standard API types doesn't work well either: https://github.com/kubernetes-sigs/controller-runtime/issues/1669
    90	//   - This leaves YAML templates, converted to unstructured types and Applied with the dynamic client.
    91	type DeploymentController struct {
    92	        client              kube.Client
    93	        clusterID           cluster.ID
    94	        env                 *model.Environment
    95	        queue               controllers.Queue
    96	        patcher             patcher
    97	        gateways            kclient.Client[*gateway.Gateway]
    98	        gatewayClasses      kclient.Client[*gateway.GatewayClass]
    99	        listenerSets        kclient.Client[*gatewayx.XListenerSet]
   100	        listenerSetByParent kclient.Index[types.NamespacedName, *gatewayx.XListenerSet]
   101	
   102	        clients         map[schema.GroupVersionResource]getter
   103	        injectConfig    func() inject.WebhookConfig
   104	        deployments     kclient.Client[*appsv1.Deployment]
   105	        services        kclient.Client[*corev1.Service]
   106	        hpas            kclient.Client[*autoscalingv2.HorizontalPodAutoscaler]
   107	        pdbs            kclient.Client[*policyv1.PodDisruptionBudget]
   108	        configMaps      kclient.Client[*corev1.ConfigMap]
   109	        serviceAccounts kclient.Client[*corev1.ServiceAccount]
   110	        namespaces      kclient.Client[*corev1.Namespace]
   111	        tagWatcher      revisions.TagWatcher
   112	        revision        string
   113	        systemNamespace string
   114	}
   115	
   116	// Patcher is a function that abstracts patching logic. This is largely because client-go fakes do not handle patching
   117	type patcher func(gvr schema.GroupVersionResource, name string, namespace string, data []byte, subresources ...string) error
   118	
   119	// classInfo holds information about a gateway class
   120	type classInfo struct {
   121	        // controller name for this class
   122	        controller string
   123	        // controller label for this class
   124	        controllerLabel string
   125	        // description for this class
   126	        description string
   127	        // The key in the templates to use for this class
   128	        templates string
   129	
   130	        // defaultServiceType sets the default service type if one is not explicit set
   131	        defaultServiceType corev1.ServiceType
   132	
   133	        // disableRouteGeneration, if set, will make it so the controller ignores this class.
   134	        disableRouteGeneration bool
   135	
   136	        // supportsListenerSet declares whether a given class supports ListenerSet
   137	        supportsListenerSet bool
   138	
   139	        // disableNameSuffix, if set, will avoid appending -<class> to names
   140	        disableNameSuffix bool
   141	
   142	        // addressType is the default address type to report
   143	        addressType gateway.AddressType
   144	}
   145	
   146	var classInfos = getClassInfos()
   147	
   148	var builtinClasses = getBuiltinClasses()
   149	
   150	func getBuiltinClasses() map[gateway.ObjectName]gateway.GatewayController {
   151	        res := map[gateway.ObjectName]gateway.GatewayController{
   152	                gateway.ObjectName(features.GatewayAPIDefaultGatewayClass): gateway.GatewayController(features.ManagedGatewayController),
   153	        }
   154	
   155	        if features.MultiNetworkGatewayAPI {
   156	                res[constants.RemoteGatewayClassName] = constants.UnmanagedGatewayController
   157	        }
   158	
   159	        if features.EnableAmbientWaypoints {
   160	                res[constants.WaypointGatewayClassName] = constants.ManagedGatewayMeshController
   161	        }
   162	
   163	        // N.B Ambient e/w gateways are just fancy waypoints, but we want a different
   164	        // GatewayClass for better UX
   165	        if features.EnableAmbientMultiNetwork {
   166	                res[constants.EastWestGatewayClassName] = constants.ManagedGatewayEastWestController
   167	        }
   168	        return res
   169	}
   170	
   171	func getClassInfos() map[gateway.GatewayController]classInfo {
   172	        m := map[gateway.GatewayController]classInfo{
   173	                gateway.GatewayController(features.ManagedGatewayController): {
   174	                        controller:          features.ManagedGatewayController,
   175	                        description:         "The default Istio GatewayClass",
   176	                        templates:           "kube-gateway",
   177	                        defaultServiceType:  corev1.ServiceTypeLoadBalancer,
   178	                        addressType:         gateway.HostnameAddressType,
   179	                        controllerLabel:     constants.ManagedGatewayControllerLabel,
   180	                        supportsListenerSet: true,
   181	                },
   182	        }
   183	
   184	        if features.MultiNetworkGatewayAPI {
   185	                m[constants.UnmanagedGatewayController] = classInfo{
   186	                        // This represents a gateway that our control plane cannot discover directly via the API server.
   187	                        // We shouldn't generate Istio resources for it. We aren't programming this gateway.
   188	                        controller:             constants.UnmanagedGatewayController,
   189	                        description:            "Remote to this cluster. Does not deploy or affect configuration.",
   190	                        disableRouteGeneration: true,
   191	                        addressType:            gateway.HostnameAddressType,
   192	                        supportsListenerSet:    false,
   193	                }
   194	        }
   195	        if features.EnableAmbientWaypoints {
   196	                m[constants.ManagedGatewayMeshController] = classInfo{
   197	                        controller:          constants.ManagedGatewayMeshController,
   198	                        description:         "The default Istio waypoint GatewayClass",
   199	                        templates:           "waypoint",
   200	                        disableNameSuffix:   true,
   201	                        defaultServiceType:  corev1.ServiceTypeClusterIP,
   202	                        supportsListenerSet: false,
   203	                        // Report both. Consumers of the gateways can choose which they want.
   204	                        // In particular, Istio across different versions consumes different address types, so this retains compat
   205	                        addressType:     "",
   206	                        controllerLabel: constants.ManagedGatewayMeshControllerLabel,
   207	                }
   208	        }
   209	
   210	        if features.EnableAmbientMultiNetwork {
   211	                m[constants.ManagedGatewayEastWestController] = classInfo{
   212	                        controller:         constants.ManagedGatewayEastWestController,
   213	                        description:        "The default GatewayClass for Istio East West Gateways",
   214	                        templates:          "waypoint",
   215	                        disableNameSuffix:  true,
   216	                        defaultServiceType: corev1.ServiceTypeLoadBalancer,
   217	                        addressType:        "",
   218	                        controllerLabel:    constants.ManagedGatewayEastWestControllerLabel,
   219	                }
   220	        }
   221	        return m
   222	}
   223	
   224	// NewDeploymentController constructs a DeploymentController and registers required informers.
   225	// The controller will not start until Run() is called.
   226	func NewDeploymentController(
   227	        client kube.Client,
   228	        clusterID cluster.ID,
   229	        env *model.Environment,
   230	        webhookConfig func() inject.WebhookConfig,
   231	        injectionHandler func(fn func()),
   232	        tw revisions.TagWatcher,
   233	        revision string,
   234	        systemNamespace string,
   235	) *DeploymentController {
   236	        filter := kclient.Filter{ObjectFilter: client.ObjectFilter()}
   237	        gateways := kclient.NewFiltered[*gateway.Gateway](client, filter)
   238	        gatewayClasses := kclient.New[*gateway.GatewayClass](client)
   239	        dc := &DeploymentController{
   240	                client:    client,
   241	                clusterID: clusterID,
   242	                clients:   map[schema.GroupVersionResource]getter{},
   243	                env:       env,
   244	                patcher: func(gvr schema.GroupVersionResource, name string, namespace string, data []byte, subresources ...string) error {
   245	                        c := client.Dynamic().Resource(gvr).Namespace(namespace)
   246	                        t := true
   247	                        _, err := c.Patch(context.Background(), name, types.ApplyPatchType, data, metav1.PatchOptions{
   248	                                Force:        &t,
   249	                                FieldManager: features.ManagedGatewayController,
   250	                        }, subresources...)
   251	                        return err
   252	                },
   253	                gateways:        gateways,
   254	                gatewayClasses:  gatewayClasses,
   255	                injectConfig:    webhookConfig,
   256	                tagWatcher:      tw,
   257	                revision:        revision,
   258	                systemNamespace: systemNamespace,
   259	        }
   260	        gatewaysByParamsRef := kclient.CreateIndex(gateways, "parametersRef", func(o *gateway.Gateway) []types.NamespacedName {
   261	                p, err := fetchParameters(o)
   262	                if p == nil || err != nil {
   263	                        return nil
   264	                }
   265	                return []types.NamespacedName{*p}
   266	        })
   267	        dc.queue = controllers.NewQueue("gateway deployment",
   268	                controllers.WithReconciler(dc.Reconcile),
   269	                controllers.WithMaxAttempts(5))
   270	
   271	        if features.EnableAlphaGatewayAPI {
   272	                dc.listenerSets = kclient.NewFiltered[*gatewayx.XListenerSet](client, filter)
   273	                dc.listenerSetByParent = kclient.CreateIndex(dc.listenerSets, "parent", func(o *gatewayx.XListenerSet) []types.NamespacedName {
   274	                        return []types.NamespacedName{extractListenerSetParent(o)}
   275	                })
   276	                dc.listenerSets.AddEventHandler(controllers.TypedObjectHandler(func(o *gatewayx.XListenerSet) {
   277	                        dc.queue.Add(extractListenerSetParent(o))
   278	                }))
   279	        }
   280	
   281	        // Set up a handler that will add the parent Gateway object onto the queue.
   282	        // The queue will only handle Gateway objects; if child resources (Service, etc) are updated we re-add
   283	        // the Gateway to the queue and reconcile the state of the world.
   284	        parentHandler := controllers.ObjectHandler(controllers.EnqueueForParentHandler(dc.queue, gvk.KubernetesGateway))
   285	
   286	        dc.services = kclient.NewFiltered[*corev1.Service](client, filter)
   287	        dc.services.AddEventHandler(parentHandler)
   288	        dc.clients[gvr.Service] = NewUntypedWrapper(dc.services)
   289	
   290	        dc.configMaps = kclient.NewFiltered[*corev1.ConfigMap](client, filter)
   291	        dc.configMaps.AddEventHandler(controllers.ObjectHandler(func(o controllers.Object) {
   292	                // This could be a configmap referenced by a Gateway paramsRef
   293	                impacted := gatewaysByParamsRef.Lookup(config.NamespacedName(o))
   294	                for _, gw := range impacted {
   295	                        dc.queue.AddObject(gw)
   296	                }
   297	                // Or it could also be a global GatewayClass config
   298	                classDefaults, classDefaultsF := o.GetLabels()[gatewayClassDefaults]
   299	                if classDefaultsF && o.GetNamespace() == dc.systemNamespace {
   300	                        for _, gw := range dc.gateways.List(metav1.NamespaceAll, klabels.Everything()) {
   301	                                if string(gw.Spec.GatewayClassName) == classDefaults {
   302	                                        dc.queue.AddObject(gw)
   303	                                }
   304	                        }
   305	                }
   306	        }))
   307	
   308	        dc.deployments = kclient.NewFiltered[*appsv1.Deployment](client, filter)
   309	        dc.deployments.AddEventHandler(parentHandler)
   310	        dc.clients[gvr.Deployment] = NewUntypedWrapper(dc.deployments)
   311	
   312	        dc.serviceAccounts = kclient.NewFiltered[*corev1.ServiceAccount](client, filter)
   313	        dc.serviceAccounts.AddEventHandler(parentHandler)
   314	        dc.clients[gvr.ServiceAccount] = NewUntypedWrapper(dc.serviceAccounts)
   315	
   316	        dc.hpas = kclient.NewFiltered[*autoscalingv2.HorizontalPodAutoscaler](client, filter)
   317	        dc.hpas.AddEventHandler(parentHandler)
   318	        dc.clients[gvr.HorizontalPodAutoscaler] = NewUntypedWrapper(dc.hpas)
   319	
   320	        dc.pdbs = kclient.NewFiltered[*policyv1.PodDisruptionBudget](client, filter)
   321	        dc.pdbs.AddEventHandler(parentHandler)
   322	        dc.clients[gvr.PodDisruptionBudget] = NewUntypedWrapper(dc.pdbs)
   323	
   324	        dc.namespaces = kclient.NewFiltered[*corev1.Namespace](client, filter)
   325	        dc.namespaces.AddEventHandler(controllers.ObjectHandler(func(o controllers.Object) {
   326	                // TODO: make this more intelligent, checking if something we care about has changed
   327	                // requeue this namespace
   328	                for _, gw := range dc.gateways.List(o.GetName(), klabels.Everything()) {
   329	                        dc.queue.AddObject(gw)
   330	                }
   331	        }))
   332	
   333	        gateways.AddEventHandler(controllers.ObjectHandler(dc.queue.AddObject))
   334	        gatewayClasses.AddEventHandler(controllers.ObjectHandler(func(o controllers.Object) {
   335	                for _, g := range dc.gateways.List(metav1.NamespaceAll, klabels.Everything()) {
   336	                        if string(g.Spec.GatewayClassName) == o.GetName() {
   337	                                dc.queue.AddObject(g)
   338	                        }
   339	                }
   340	        }))
   341	
   342	        // On injection template change, requeue all gateways
   343	        injectionHandler(func() {
   344	                for _, gw := range dc.gateways.List(metav1.NamespaceAll, klabels.Everything()) {
   345	                        dc.queue.AddObject(gw)
   346	                }
   347	        })
   348	
   349	        dc.tagWatcher.AddHandler(dc.HandleTagChange)
   350	
   351	        return dc
   352	}
   353	
   354	func extractListenerSetParent(o *gatewayx.XListenerSet) types.NamespacedName {
   355	        n := o.Spec.ParentRef.Name
   356	        ns := ptr.OrDefault(o.Spec.ParentRef.Namespace, gatewayx.Namespace(o.Namespace))
   357	        return types.NamespacedName{
   358	                Namespace: string(ns),
   359	                Name:      string(n),
   360	        }
   361	}
   362	
   363	func (d *DeploymentController) Run(stop <-chan struct{}) {
   364	        kube.WaitForCacheSync(
   365	                "deployment controller",
   366	                stop,
   367	                d.namespaces.HasSynced,
   368	                d.deployments.HasSynced,
   369	                d.services.HasSynced,
   370	                d.configMaps.HasSynced,
   371	                d.serviceAccounts.HasSynced,
   372	                d.hpas.HasSynced,
   373	                d.pdbs.HasSynced,
   374	                d.gateways.HasSynced,
   375	                d.gatewayClasses.HasSynced,
   376	                d.tagWatcher.HasSynced,
   377	        )
   378	        d.queue.Run(stop)
   379	        controllers.ShutdownAll(
   380	                d.namespaces,
   381	                d.deployments,
   382	                d.services,
   383	                d.configMaps,
   384	                d.serviceAccounts,
   385	                d.hpas,
   386	                d.pdbs,
   387	                d.gateways,
   388	                d.gatewayClasses,
   389	        )
   390	}
   391	
   392	// Reconcile takes in the name of a Gateway and ensures the cluster is in the desired state
   393	func (d *DeploymentController) Reconcile(req types.NamespacedName) error {
   394	        log := log.WithLabels("gateway", req)
   395	
   396	        gw := d.gateways.Get(req.Name, req.Namespace)
   397	        if gw == nil {
   398	                log.Debugf("gateway no longer exists")
   399	                // we'll ignore not-found errors, since they can't be fixed by an immediate
   400	                // requeue (we'll need to wait for a new notification), and we can get them
   401	                // on deleted requests.
   402	                return nil
   403	        }
   404	
   405	        var controller gateway.GatewayController
   406	        if gc := d.gatewayClasses.Get(string(gw.Spec.GatewayClassName), ""); gc != nil {
   407	                controller = gc.Spec.ControllerName
   408	        } else {
   409	                if builtin, f := builtinClasses[gw.Spec.GatewayClassName]; f {

    38	// Object is a union of runtime + meta objects. Essentially every k8s object meets this interface.
    39	// and certainly all that we care about.
    40	type Object interface {
    41	        metav1.Object
    42	        runtime.Object
    43	}

    45	type ComparableObject interface {
    46	        comparable
    47	        Object
    48	}

    50	// IsNil works around comparing generic types
    51	func IsNil[O comparable](o O) bool {
    52	        var t O
    53	        return o == t
    54	}

    56	// UnstructuredToGVR extracts the GVR of an unstructured resource. This is useful when using dynamic
    57	// clients.
    58	func UnstructuredToGVR(u unstructured.Unstructured) (schema.GroupVersionResource, error) {
    59	        res := schema.GroupVersionResource{}
    60	        gv, err := schema.ParseGroupVersion(u.GetAPIVersion())
    61	        if err != nil {
    62	                return res, err
    63	        }
    64	
    65	        gk := config.GroupVersionKind{
    66	                Group:   gv.Group,
    67	                Version: gv.Version,
    68	                Kind:    u.GetKind(),
    69	        }
    70	        found, ok := gvk.ToGVR(gk)
    71	        if !ok {
    72	                return res, fmt.Errorf("unknown gvk: %v", gk)
    73	        }
    74	        return found, nil
    75	}
    76	
    77	// ObjectToGVR extracts the GVR of an unstructured resource. This is useful when using dynamic
    78	// clients.
    79	func ObjectToGVR(u Object) (schema.GroupVersionResource, error) {
    80	        g := u.GetObjectKind().GroupVersionKind()
    81	
    82	        gk := config.GroupVersionKind{
    83	                Group:   g.Group,
    84	                Version: g.Version,
    85	                Kind:    g.Kind,
    86	        }
    87	        found, ok := gvk.ToGVR(gk)
    88	        if !ok {
    89	                return schema.GroupVersionResource{}, fmt.Errorf("unknown gvk: %v", gk)
    90	        }
    91	        return found, nil
    92	}

    94	// EnqueueForParentHandler returns a handler that will enqueue the parent (by ownerRef) resource
    95	func EnqueueForParentHandler(q Queue, kind config.GroupVersionKind) func(obj Object) {
    96	        handler := func(obj Object) {
    97	                for _, ref := range obj.GetOwnerReferences() {
    98	                        refGV, err := schema.ParseGroupVersion(ref.APIVersion)
    99	                        if err != nil {
   100	                                log.Errorf("could not parse OwnerReference api version %q: %v", ref.APIVersion, err)
   101	                                continue
   102	                        }
   103	                        if refGV.Group == kind.Group && ref.Kind == kind.Kind {
   104	                                // We found a parent we care about, add it to the queue
   105	                                q.Add(types.NamespacedName{
   106	                                        // Reference doesn't have namespace, but its always same-namespace, so use objects
   107	                                        Namespace: obj.GetNamespace(),
   108	                                        Name:      ref.Name,
   109	                                })
   110	                        }
   111	                }
   112	        }
   113	        return handler
   114	}
   115	
   116	// EventType represents a registry update event
   117	type EventType int
   118	
   119	const (
   120	        // EventAdd is sent when an object is added
   121	        EventAdd EventType = iota
   122	
   123	        // EventUpdate is sent when an object is modified
   124	        // Captures the modified object
   125	        EventUpdate
   126	
   127	        // EventDelete is sent when an object is deleted
   128	        // Captures the object at the last known state
   129	        EventDelete
   130	)
   131	
   132	func (event EventType) String() string {
   133	        out := "unknown"
   134	        switch event {
   135	        case EventAdd:
   136	                out = "add"
   137	        case EventUpdate:
   138	                out = "update"
   139	        case EventDelete:
   140	                out = "delete"
   141	        }
   142	        return out
   143	}
   144	
   145	type Event struct {
   146	        Old   Object
   147	        New   Object
   148	        Event EventType
   149	}
   150	
   151	func (e Event) Latest() Object {
   152	        if e.New != nil {
   153	                return e.New
   154	        }
   155	        return e.Old
   156	}
   157	
   158	func FromEventHandler(handler func(o Event)) cache.ResourceEventHandler {
   159	        return cache.ResourceEventHandlerFuncs{
   160	                AddFunc: func(obj any) {
   161	                        o := ExtractObject(obj)
   162	                        if o == nil {
   163	                                return
   164	                        }
   165	                        handler(Event{
   166	                                New:   o,
   167	                                Event: EventAdd,
   168	                        })
   169	                },
   170	                UpdateFunc: func(oldInterface, newInterface any) {
   171	                        oldObj := ExtractObject(oldInterface)
   172	                        if oldObj == nil {
   173	                                return
   174	                        }
   175	                        newObj := ExtractObject(newInterface)
   176	                        if newObj == nil {
   177	                                return
   178	                        }
   179	                        handler(Event{
   180	                                Old:   oldObj,
   181	                                New:   newObj,
   182	                                Event: EventUpdate,
   183	                        })
   184	                },
   185	                DeleteFunc: func(obj any) {
   186	                        o := ExtractObject(obj)
   187	                        if o == nil {
   188	                                return
   189	                        }
   190	                        handler(Event{
   191	                                Old:   o,
   192	                                Event: EventDelete,
   193	                        })
   194	                },
   195	        }
   196	}
   197	
   198	// ObjectHandler returns a handler that will act on the latest version of an object
   199	// This means Add/Update/Delete are all handled the same and are just used to trigger reconciling.
   200	func ObjectHandler(handler func(o Object)) cache.ResourceEventHandler {
   201	        return TypedObjectHandler[Object](handler)
   202	}
   203	
   204	func TypedObjectHandler[T ComparableObject](handler func(o T)) cache.ResourceEventHandler {
   205	        h := func(obj any) {
   206	                o := Extract[T](obj)
   207	                if IsNil(o) {
   208	                        return
   209	                }
   210	                handler(o)
   211	        }
   212	        return cache.ResourceEventHandlerFuncs{
   213	                AddFunc: h,
   214	                UpdateFunc: func(oldObj, newObj any) {
   215	                        h(newObj)
   216	                },
   217	                DeleteFunc: h,
   218	        }
   219	}
   220	
   221	// FilteredObjectHandler returns a handler that will act on the latest version of an object
   222	// This means Add/Update/Delete are all handled the same and are just used to trigger reconciling.
   223	// If filters are set, returning 'false' will exclude the event. For Add and Deletes, the filter will be based
   224	// on the new or old item. For updates, the item will be handled if either the new or the old object is updated.
   225	func FilteredObjectHandler(handler func(o Object), filter func(o Object) bool) cache.ResourceEventHandler {
   226	        return filteredObjectHandler(handler, false, filter)
   227	}
   228	
   229	// FilteredObjectSpecHandler returns a handler that will act on the latest version of an object
   230	// This means Add/Update/Delete are all handled the same and are just used to trigger reconciling.
   231	// Unlike FilteredObjectHandler, the handler is only trigger when the resource spec changes (ie resourceVersion)
   232	// If filters are set, returning 'false' will exclude the event. For Add and Deletes, the filter will be based
   233	// on the new or old item. For updates, the item will be handled if either the new or the old object is updated.
   234	func FilteredObjectSpecHandler(handler func(o Object), filter func(o Object) bool) cache.ResourceEventHandler {
   235	        return filteredObjectHandler(handler, true, filter)
   236	}
   237	
   238	func filteredObjectHandler(handler func(o Object), onlyIncludeSpecChanges bool, filter func(o Object) bool) cache.ResourceEventHandler {
   239	        single := func(obj any) {
   240	                o := ExtractObject(obj)
   241	                if o == nil {
   242	                        return
   243	                }
   244	                if !filter(o) {
   245	                        return
   246	                }
   247	                handler(o)
   248	        }
   249	        return cache.ResourceEventHandlerFuncs{
   250	                AddFunc: single,
   251	                UpdateFunc: func(oldInterface, newInterface any) {
   252	                        oldObj := ExtractObject(oldInterface)
   253	                        if oldObj == nil {
   254	                                return
   255	                        }
   256	                        newObj := ExtractObject(newInterface)
   257	                        if newObj == nil {
   258	                                return
   259	                        }
   260	                        if onlyIncludeSpecChanges && oldObj.GetResourceVersion() == newObj.GetResourceVersion() {
   261	                                return
   262	                        }
   263	                        newer := filter(newObj)
   264	                        older := filter(oldObj)
   265	                        if !newer && !older {
   266	                                return
   267	                        }
   268	                        handler(newObj)
   269	                },
   270	                DeleteFunc: single,
   271	        }
   272	}
   273	
   274	// Extract pulls a T from obj, handling tombstones.
   275	// This will return nil if the object cannot be extracted.
   276	func Extract[T Object](obj any) T {
   277	        var empty T
   278	        if obj == nil {
   279	                return empty
   280	        }
   281	        o, ok := obj.(T)
   282	        if !ok {
   283	                tombstone, ok := obj.(cache.DeletedFinalStateUnknown)
   284	                if !ok {
   285	                        log.Errorf("couldn't get object from tombstone: (%T vs %T) %+v", obj, ptr.Empty[T](), obj)
   286	                        return empty
   287	                }
   288	                o, ok = tombstone.Obj.(T)
   289	                if !ok {
   290	                        log.Errorf("tombstone contained object that is not an object (key:%v, obj:%T)", tombstone.Key, tombstone.Obj)
   291	                        return empty
   292	                }
   293	        }
   294	        return o
   295	}
   296	
   297	func ExtractObject(obj any) Object {
   298	        return Extract[Object](obj)
   299	}
   300	
   301	// IgnoreNotFound returns nil on NotFound errors.
   302	// All other values that are not NotFound errors or nil are returned unmodified.
   303	func IgnoreNotFound(err error) error {
   304	        if kerrors.IsNotFound(err) {
   305	                return nil
   306	        }
   307	        return err
   308	}
   309	
   310	// EventHandler mirrors ResourceEventHandlerFuncs, but takes typed T objects instead of any.
   311	type EventHandler[T Object] struct {
   312	        AddFunc         func(obj T)
   313	        AddExtendedFunc func(obj T, initialSync bool)
   314	        UpdateFunc      func(oldObj, newObj T)
   315	        DeleteFunc      func(obj T)
   316	}
   317	
   318	func (e EventHandler[T]) OnAdd(obj interface{}, initialSync bool) {
   319	        if e.AddExtendedFunc != nil {
   320	                e.AddExtendedFunc(Extract[T](obj), initialSync)
   321	        } else if e.AddFunc != nil {
   322	                e.AddFunc(Extract[T](obj))
   323	        }
   324	}
   325	
   326	func (e EventHandler[T]) OnUpdate(oldObj, newObj interface{}) {
   327	        if e.UpdateFunc != nil {
   328	                e.UpdateFunc(Extract[T](oldObj), Extract[T](newObj))
   329	        }
   330	}
   331	
   332	func (e EventHandler[T]) OnDelete(obj interface{}) {
   333	        if e.DeleteFunc != nil {
   334	                e.DeleteFunc(Extract[T](obj))
   335	        }
   336	}
   337	
   338	var _ cache.ResourceEventHandler = EventHandler[Object]{}
   339	
   340	type Shutdowner interface {
   341	        ShutdownHandlers()
   342	}
   343	
   344	// ShutdownAll is a simple helper to shutdown all informers
   345	func ShutdownAll(s ...Shutdowner) {
   346	        for _, h := range s {
   347	                h.ShutdownHandlers()
   348	        }
   349	}
   350	
   351	func OldestObject[T Object](configs []T) T {
   352	        return slices.MinFunc(configs, func(i, j T) int {
   353	                if r := i.GetCreationTimestamp().Compare(j.GetCreationTimestamp().Time); r != 0 {
   354	                        return r
   355	                }
   356	                // If creation time is the same, then behavior is nondeterministic. In this case, we can
   357	                // pick an arbitrary but consistent ordering based on name and namespace, which is unique.
   358	                // CreationTimestamp is stored in seconds, so this is not uncommon.
   359	                if r := cmp.Compare(i.GetName(), j.GetName()); r != 0 {
   360	                        return r
   361	                }
   362	                return cmp.Compare(i.GetNamespace(), j.GetNamespace())
   363	        })
   364	}

import (
	"fmt"
	"reflect"

	gateway "sigs.k8s.io/gateway-api/apis/v1beta1"
)

func main() {
	// Create two gateway objects with same spec but different status
	gw1 := &gateway.Gateway{
		Spec: gateway.GatewaySpec{
			GatewayClassName: "test-class",
		},
		Status: gateway.GatewayStatus{
			Addresses: []gateway.GatewayStatusAddress{
				{Value: "10.0.0.1"},
			},
		},
	}

	gw2 := &gateway.Gateway{
		Spec: gateway.GatewaySpec{
			GatewayClassName: "test-class",
		},
		Status: gateway.GatewayStatus{
			Addresses: []gateway.GatewayStatusAddress{
				{Value: "10.0.0.2"},
			},
		},
	}

	// Check if specs are equal
	fmt.Printf("Specs equal: %v\n", reflect.DeepEqual(gw1.Spec, gw2.Spec))
	fmt.Printf("Objects equal: %v\n", reflect.DeepEqual(gw1, gw2))
	fmt.Printf("Status equal: %v\n", reflect.DeepEqual(gw1.Status, gw2.Status))
}
'

func (e EventHandler[T]) OnAdd(obj interface{}, initialSync bool) {
	if e.AddExtendedFunc != nil {
		e.AddExtendedFunc(Extract[T](obj), initialSync)
	} else if e.AddFunc != nil {
		e.AddFunc(Extract[T](obj))
	}
}

func (e EventHandler[T]) OnUpdate(oldObj, newObj interface{}) {
	if e.UpdateFunc != nil {
		e.UpdateFunc(Extract[T](oldObj), Extract[T](newObj))
	}
}

func (e EventHandler[T]) OnDelete(obj interface{}) {
	if e.DeleteFunc != nil {
		e.DeleteFunc(Extract[T](obj))
	}
}

var _ cache.ResourceEventHandler = EventHandler[Object]{}

type Shutdowner interface {
	ShutdownHandlers()
}

// ShutdownAll is a simple helper to shutdown all informers
func ShutdownAll(s ...Shutdowner) {
	for _, h := range s {
		h.ShutdownHandlers()
	}
}

   159	        return cache.ResourceEventHandlerFuncs{
   160	                AddFunc: func(obj any) {
   161	                        o := ExtractObject(obj)
   162	                        if o == nil {
   163	                                return
   164	                        }
   165	                        handler(Event{
   166	                                New:   o,
   167	                                Event: EventAdd,
   168	                        })
   169	                },
   170	                UpdateFunc: func(oldInterface, newInterface any) {
   171	                        oldObj := ExtractObject(oldInterface)
   172	                        if oldObj == nil {
   173	                                return
   174	                        }
   175	                        newObj := ExtractObject(newInterface)
   176	                        if newObj == nil {
   177	                                return
   178	                        }

   180	                                Old:   oldObj,

   182	                                Event: EventUpdate,
   183	                        })

   186	                        o := ExtractObject(obj)
   187	                        if o == nil {
   188	                                return
   189	                        }
   190	                        handler(Event{
   191	                                Old:   o,
   192	                                Event: EventDelete,
   193	                        })
   194	                },
   195	        }
   196	}
   197	
   198	// ObjectHandler returns a handler that will act on the latest version of an object
   199	// This means Add/Update/Delete are all handled the same and are just used to trigger reconciling.
   200	func ObjectHandler(handler func(o Object)) cache.ResourceEventHandler {
   201	        return TypedObjectHandler[Object](handler)
   202	}
   203	
   204	func TypedObjectHandler[T ComparableObject](handler func(o T)) cache.ResourceEventHandler {
   205	        h := func(obj any) {
   206	                o := Extract[T](obj)
   207	                if IsNil(o) {
   208	                        return
   209	                }
   210	                handler(o)
   211	        }
   212	        return cache.ResourceEventHandlerFuncs{
   213	                AddFunc: h,
   214	                UpdateFunc: func(oldObj, newObj any) {
   215	                        h(newObj)
   216	                },
   217	                DeleteFunc: h,
   218	        }
   219	}
